</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Highlights Long-Term Growth Strategy in Asia Pacific, Middle East&nbsp;&amp;
Africa (AMEA) Region at 2022 CAGNY Conference </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">With #1 Position in Packaged Snacks and Strong Local-First Capabilities, Region Represents Powerful Long-Term
Growth Engine </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CHICAGO, February</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;22, 2022</B> &#150; Mondel&#275;z International (Nasdaq: MDLZ) will today
spotlight its strategy for the Asia Pacific, Middle East&nbsp;&amp; Africa (AMEA) region at the 2022 Consumer Analyst Group of New York (CAGNY) Conference. Dirk Van de Put, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, and Maurizio Brusadelli, Executive
Vice President&nbsp;&amp; President, AMEA, will detail the attractive growth opportunities in this large and diverse region, as well as key strategic initiatives designed to advance sustainable growth and create shareholder value. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our performance in the AMEA region provides a strong example of Mondel&#275;z International&#146;s virtuous cycle in action,&#148; said Van de Put.
&#147;We have become the #1 packaged snacks company in the region<FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"> as a
result of a focused reinvestment strategy enabling consistent, volume-driven organic revenue growth, strong profitability and increased share gains over several years. We see significant opportunities ahead, and we are excited about our long-term
growth prospects in the region.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Unique Portfolio of Iconic Global Brands and Local Jewels </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International offers market-leading brands in key geographies that drive its success in the region. Ninety percent of AMEA revenue comes from
focus brands, including two $1&nbsp;billion global brands in <I>Oreo </I>and <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk</I>, as well as 11 brands with revenues of more than $100&nbsp;million, including local jewels such as<I> </I><I>Bournvita</I> and <I>Kinh</I><I>
Do.</I> </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s long history in the region &#150; combined with its local-first strategy, robust supply
chain, sophisticated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">route-to-market</FONT></FONT> infrastructure and high levels of investment &#150; represent key competitive advantages. The AMEA region has delivered robust
growth, averaging <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digits over the past three years, underpinned by strong volume growth, healthy pricing and continued productivity gains. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;With operations in 27 countries and sales in more than 70 markets, Mondel&#275;z International is a clear leader in packaged snacks in AMEA, and we are
continuing to gain share,&#148; added Brusadelli. &#147;Our unique combination of strong positions across key markets, a proven track record and sustainable competitive advantage give us great confidence in our ability to accelerate growth in AMEA
for many years to come. Additionally, the resilience shown by our team during the last few years showcases our winning culture and our ability to manage through volatility.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Significant Long-Term Growth Prospects in AMEA </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At the
conference, Brusadelli will outline the company&#146;s AMEA strategy, providing further detail on its plans to accelerate revenue and share gains in the region by prioritizing: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International will also showcase its business in India and China &#150; two of the region&#146;s fastest-growing markets &#150; to highlight the

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
